Based on U.S. GAAP guidance, the bank has adopted the liquidation basis of accounting for the March close. The transition from a going concern basis of accounting to a liquidation basis of accounting has resulted in the recognition of $8.6 million of net interest income, $10.9 million of additional impairments of securities, and $69.8 million of non-interest expenses. This has resulted in a reduction in equity of $72.1 million. On a going concern basis, the bank's tier 1 leverage capital ratio would have been 4.76.
